#### position.md

**Title:** Position

**Path:** `styles/position.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Position

The `position` style determines the reference point for [`offset`](./offset.md).  
Default: `"relative"` — applies offset to the widget’s normal position.  
Example: `offset=(1, 1)` moves the widget 1 cell and 1 line down from its default location.

Alternative: `"absolute"` — applies offset relative to container origin (top-left corner).  
Example: `offset=(1, 1)` places the widget 1 cell and 1 line from the top-left.

!!! note

    Absolute positioning overrides parent alignment rules.

## Syntax

--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"
position: <a href="../../css_types/position">&lt;position&gt;</a>;
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

## Examples

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/position.py"}
    ```

=== "position.py"

    ```py
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/position.py"
    ```

=== "position.tcss"

    ```css
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/position.tcss"
    ```

## CSS

```css
position: relative;
position: absolute;
```

## Python

```py
widget.styles.position = "relative"
widget.styles.position = "absolute"
```

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_py`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/position.py"
    
```

    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/position.tcss"

```

### `inline_py`

```

```text
# Scrollbar Colors

Customize scrollbar appearance via CSS styles. Default themes provide optimized colors; override only when needed.

| Style                        | Applies to |
|------------------------------|------------|
| `scrollbar-background`       | Scrollbar background |
| `scrollbar-background-active`| Background during drag |
| `scrollbar-background-hover` | Background on hover |
| `scrollbar-color`            | Thumb (movable part) |
| `scrollbar-color-active`     | Thumb during drag |
| `scrollbar-color-hover`      | Thumb on hover |
| `scrollbar-corner-color`     | Corner gap between scrollbars |

## Syntax

```css
scrollbar-background: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-background-active: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-background-hover: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-color: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-color-active: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-color-hover: <color> [<percentage>];
scrollbar-corner-color: <color> [<percentage>];
```

Each value accepts a `<color>` and optional `<percentage>` (opacity). Refer to individual style docs for usage details.

## Example

Two panels with oversized text. Right panel uses custom scrollbars; left shows defaults.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/scrollbars.py"}
    ```

=== "scrollbars.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbars.py"

**Content:**

```text
# Scrollbar-gutter

The `scrollbar-gutter` style reserves space for a vertical scrollbar.

## Syntax

--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"
scrollbar-gutter: auto | stable;
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

### Values

| Value     | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| `auto`    | No space reserved; layout recalculates when scrollbar appears. |
| `stable`  | Space reserved; prevents layout shifts when scrollbar becomes visible. |

## Example

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_gutter.py"}
    ```

=== "scrollbar_gutter.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_gutter.py"
    ```

=== "scrollbar_gutter.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="2"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_gutter.tcss"
    ```

## CSS

```css
scrollbar-gutter: auto;    /* No space reserved for vertical scrollbar. */
scrollbar-gutter: stable;  /* Space reserved to prevent layout shifts. */
```

## Python

```python
self.styles.scrollbar_gutter = "auto"    # No space reserved.
self.styles.scrollbar_gutter = "stable"  # Space reserved.
```

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_gutter.py"
    
```

### `inline_css`

```
scrollbar-gutter: auto;    /* Don't reserve space for a vertical scrollbar. */
scrollbar-gutter: stable;  /* Reserve space for a vertical scrollbar. */

```

### `inline_python`

```
self.styles.scrollbar_gutter = "auto"    # Don't reserve space for a vertical scrollbar.
self.styles.scrollbar_gutter = "stable"  # Reserve space for a vertical scrollbar.

```

```

#### scrollbar_size.md

**Title:** Scrollbar-size

**Path:** `styles/scrollbar_size.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Scrollbar-size

The `scrollbar-size` style defines the width of scrollbars.

## Syntax

```css
scrollbar-size: <integer> <integer>; /* horizontal vertical */
scrollbar-size-horizontal: <integer>;
scrollbar-size-vertical: <integer>;
```

Sets horizontal and vertical scrollbar widths, respectively. Scrollbar length is always 100% of container height/width.

Individual sizing via `scrollbar-size-horizontal` and `scrollbar-size-vertical`.

## Examples

### Basic usage

Modifies widget scrollbar to be significantly larger.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size.py"}
    ```

=== "scrollbar_size.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size.py"
    ```

=== "scrollbar_size.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="13"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size.tcss"
    ```

### Scrollbar sizes comparison

Three containers with distinct scrollbar widths.

!!! tip
    Set size to `0` to hide scrollbar while preserving scroll functionality via mousewheel or keyboard.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size2.py"}
    ```

=== "scrollbar_size2.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size2.py"
    ```

=== "scrollbar_size2.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="6 11 16"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/scrollbar_size2.tcss"
    ```

## CSS

```css
/* Set horizontal scrollbar to 10, vertical to 4 */
scrollbar-size: 10 4;

/* Individual sizing */
scrollbar-size-horizontal: 10;
scrollbar-size-vertical: 4;
```

## Python

No direct `scrollbar-size` equivalent. Use:

```py
# Horizontal scrollbar size
widget.styles.scrollbar_size_horizontal = 10

# Vertical scrollbar size
widget.styles.scrollbar_size_vertical = 4
```

```

# Scrollbar Visibility

Controls visibility of scrollbars in a container.

When `hidden`, scrollbars are not rendered, but scrolling via mouse wheel, keyboard, or gestures remains functional.

## Syntax

--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"
scrollbar-visibility: hidden | visible;
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

### Values

| Value         | Description                          |
|---------------|--------------------------------------|
| `hidden`      | Hides scrollbars.                    |
| `visible` (default) | Displays scrollbars normally. |

## Examples

Two containers with identical content; right container has hidden scrollbars.

```text
# Text-opacity

The `text-opacity` style blends foreground text color with background color.

## Syntax

--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"
text-opacity: <a href="../../css_types/number">&lt;number&gt;</a> | <a href="../../css_types/percentage">&lt;percentage&gt;</a>;
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

Values range from `0` (invisible text) to `1` or `100%` (fully opaque).  
- `<number>`: `0.0` to `1.0`  
- `<percentage>`: `0%` to `100%`

Typical values are between extremes; e.g., `70%` yields slightly faded text, `0.3` produces very dim text.

!!! warning

    Avoid excessively low values that impair readability.

## Example

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/text_opacity.py"}
    ```

=== "text_opacity.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_opacity.py"

    ```css hl_lines="2 6 10 14 18"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_opacity.tcss"
    ```

```

## Python

```python

```

## See also

 - [`opacity`](./opacity.md) for full-widget transparency control.

#### text_overflow.md

**Title:** Text-overflow

**Path:** `styles/text_overflow.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Text-overflow

Defines behavior when text overflows its container.

Overflow occurs when text cannot fit within the available width, due to disabled wrapping (`text-wrap`) or excessively long words.

### Syntax  
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"  
text-overflow: clip | fold | ellipsis;  
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

### Values

| Value      | Description                                                                 |
|------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `clip`     | Truncates overflow text (removed from output).                              |
| `fold`     | Wraps overflowing text to next line(s), without respecting word boundaries.  |
| `ellipsis` | Truncates text and replaces last visible character with an ellipsis.         |

### Example

Demonstrates all three values with disabled `text-wrap`, causing overflow.

- **clip**: Text clipped; single-line output.
- **fold**: Overflow wraps to next line(s); words may break across lines.
- **ellipsis**: Truncated text ends with ellipsis, indicating potential hidden content.

=== "Output"  
    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/text_overflow.py"}  

=== "text_overflow.py"  
    ```py
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_overflow.py"

=== "text_overflow.tcss"  
    ```css
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_overflow.tcss"

### CSS  
```css
#widget {
    text-overflow: ellipsis;
}

### Python  
```py
widget.styles.text_overflow = "ellipsis"
```

## See also

- [`text-wrap`](./text_wrap.md) – controls wrapping behavior.

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_py`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_overflow.py"
    
```

### `inline_css`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/text_overflow.tcss"
    
```

### `inline_css`

```

    text-overflow: ellipsis;
}

```

### `inline_py`

```

```

#### tint.md

**Title:** Tint

**Path:** `styles/tint.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Tint

The `tint` style blends a color with the entire widget.

## Syntax

--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_start.md"
tint: <a href="../../css_types/color">&lt;color&gt;</a> [<a href="../../css_types/percentage">&lt;percentage&gt;</a>];
--8<-- "docs/snippets/syntax_block_end.md"

Applies a color blend to the widget, where `<color>` may include alpha via direct specification or optional `<percentage>`. Without alpha, content is obscured.

## Example

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/tint.py"}
    ```

=== "tint.py"

    ```python hl_lines="13"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/tint.py"
    ```

    1. Tint uses `Color.with_alpha()` to vary opacity.

=== "tint.tcss"

    ```css
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/tint.tcss"
    ```

## CSS

```css
/* Red tint (e.g., error indicator) */
tint: red 20%;

/* Green tint */
tint: rgba(0, 200, 0, 0.3);
```

## Python

```python
# Red tint
from textual.color import Color
widget.styles.tint = Color.parse("red").with_alpha(0.2);

# Green tint
widget.styles.tint = "rgba(0, 200, 0, 0.3)";
```

> **Note**: Limit input size for API calls.

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_css`

#### visibility.md

**Title:** Visibility

**Path:** `styles/visibility.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Visibility

The `visibility` style controls whether a widget is rendered.

## Syntax

```css
visibility: hidden | visible;
```

### Values

| Value       | Description                          |
|-------------|--------------------------------------|
| `hidden`    | Widget is not rendered (invisible).  |
| `visible`   | Widget is rendered normally (default). |

### Inheritance

Children inherit parent visibility by default. An invisible container’s children are hidden unless explicitly set to `visibility: visible`.

## Examples

### Basic Usage

Second widget is hidden, but space remains.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/visibility.py"}
    ```

=== "visibility.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility.py"
    ```

=== "visibility.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="14"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility.tcss"
    ```

### Overriding Container Visibility

Three rows, each with a `Horizontal` container and three placeholders.  
- Top: visible (white background shown).  
- Middle: invisible; children inherit visibility.  
- Bottom: invisible but children override via explicit `visibility: visible`.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/visibility_containers.py"}
    ```

=== "visibility_containers.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility_containers.py"
    ```

=== "visibility_containers.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="2-3 7 9-11 13-15 17-19"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility_containers.tcss"
    ```

## CSS

```css
/* Invisible */
visibility: hidden;

/* Visible */
visibility: visible;
```

## Python

```python
# Set via styles
self.styles.visibility = "hidden"  # invisible
self.styles.visibility = "visible"  # visible

# Shortcut property
widget.visible = False  # invisible
widget.visible = True   # visible
```

## See also

- [`display`](./display.md) – controls whether a widget is laid out and rendered.

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/visibility_containers.py"
    
```

### `inline_css`

```
/* Widget is invisible */
visibility: hidden;

/* Widget is visible */
visibility: visible;

```

### `inline_python`

```
# Widget is invisible
self.styles.visibility = "hidden"

# Widget is visible
self.styles.visibility = "visible"

```

### `inline_python`

```
# Make a widget invisible
widget.visible = False

# Make the widget visible again
widget.visible = True

```

#### width.md

**Title:** Width

**Path:** `styles/width.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Width

The `width` style sets a widget's horizontal dimension.

## Syntax

```css
width: <scalar>;
```

Applies a `<scalar>` value to define the width. By default, this controls the content area; when [`box-sizing`](./box_sizing.md) is `border-box`, it governs the border box area.

## Examples

### Basic Usage

Sets widget width to 50% of screen:

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/width.py"}
    ```

=== "width.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/width.py"
    ```

=== "width.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="3"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/width.tcss"
    ```

### All Width Formats

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/styles/width_comparison.py" lines=24 columns=80}
    ```

=== "width_comparison.py"

    ```py hl_lines="15-23"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/width_comparison.py"
    ```

    1. ID of placeholder determines unit used for width.

=== "width_comparison.tcss"

    ```css hl_lines="2 5 8 11 14 17 20 23 26"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/width_comparison.tcss"
    ```

    1. Width = 9 columns  
    2. Width = 12.5% of container (80 cols → 10)  
    3. Width = 10% of direct parent (`Horizontal`, 80 cols → 8)  
    4. Width = 25% of `Horizontal` height (24 rows → 6)  
    5. Width = 15% of viewport width (80 cols → 12)  
    6. Width = 25% of viewport height (24 rows → 6)  
    7. Width = auto: optimal fit for content (`"#auto"` → 5 chars)  
    8. Width = `1fr`: one-third the width of a `3fr` placeholder  
    9. Width = `3fr`: triple the width of a `1fr` placeholder

## CSS

```css
/* Cell width */
width: 10;

/* Percentage (container-relative) */
width: 50%;

/* Automatic fit */
width: auto;
```

## Python

```python
widget.styles.width = 10
widget.styles.width = "50%"
widget.styles.width = "auto"
```

## See Also

- [`max-width`](./max_width.md), [`min-width`](./min_width.md) to constrain width  
- [`height`](./height.md) for vertical sizing

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/styles/width.py"
    
```

### `inline_css`

```
/* Explicit cell width */
width: 10;

/* Percentage width */
width: 50%;

/* Automatic width */
width: auto;

```

### `inline_python`

```
widget.styles.width = 10
widget.styles.width = "50%
widget.styles.width = "auto"

```

#### collapsible.md

**Title:** Collapsible

**Path:** `widgets/collapsible.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Collapsible

!!! tip "Added in version 0.37"

A focusable container with a title that toggles visibility of its content via click or `Enter` keypress.

## Composing

Content added via constructor children or context manager (`with`):

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    yield Collapsible(Label("Hello, world."))
```

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    with Collapsible():
        yield Label("Hello, world.")
```

Preferred: `with` syntax; equivalent result.

## Title

Customize via `title` parameter:

```python
with Collapsible(title="An interesting story."):
    yield Label("Interesting but verbose story.")
```

## Initial State

Control initial state with `collapsed` (`True` = collapsed, `False` = expanded):

```python
with Collapsible(title="Contents 1", collapsed=False):
    yield Label("Hello, world.")

with Collapsible(title="Contents 2", collapsed=True):  # Default
    yield Label("Hello, world.")
```

## Symbols

Customize collapse/expand symbols using `collapsed_symbol` and `expanded_symbol`:

```python
with Collapsible(collapsed_symbol=">>>", expanded_symbol="v"):
    yield Label("Hello, world.")
```

## Examples

### Three States (All Expanded, All Collapsed, Mixed)
```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/collapsible.py" press="e"}
```
```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/collapsible.py" press="c"}
```
```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/collapsible.py"}
```

### Nested Collapsibles (Initial State)
```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/collapsible_nested.py"}
```

### Custom Symbols
```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/collapsible_custom_symbol.py"}
```

## Reactive Attributes

| Name        | Type   | Default  | Description                          |
|-------------|--------|----------|--------------------------------------|
| `collapsed` | `bool` | `True`   | Controls collapsed/expanded state. |
| `title`     | `str`  | `"Toggle"` | Title of the widget.               |

## Messages

- [Collapsible.Toggled][textual.widgets.Collapsible.Toggled]

## Bindings

Defined on title:  
::: textual.widgets._collapsible.CollapsibleTitle.BINDINGS
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

## Component Classes

::: textual.widgets.Collapsible
    options:
      heading_level: 2

#### data_table.md

**Title:** DataTable

**Path:** `widgets/data_table.md`

**Content:**

```text
# DataTable

A focusable widget for efficient display and interaction with tabular data. Supports dynamic updates, cursor navigation, mouse events, row/column deletion, and per-cell Rich renderables.

## Overview

- **Focusable**: Yes  
- **Container**: No  

Emits events for selection, highlighting, and user interactions. Supports custom formatting, filtering, search repopulation, and reactive logic via `cursor_type`, `hover_coordinate`, and `cursor_coordinate`.

---

### Adding Data

Define columns with [`add_columns`](textual.widgets.DataTable.add_columns), then populate rows using [`add_rows`](textual.widgets.DataTable.add_rows).  
Single additions: use [`add_row`](textual.widgets.DataTable.add_row) or [`add_column`](textual.widgets.DataTable.add_column).

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table.py"
```

---

### Styling & Cell Rendering

Cells support Rich renderables (e.g., `Text`). Use `Text` for styled, justified content.

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_renderables.py"
```

---

### Keys

Each row and column may have a unique `key`.  
- If omitted, Textual auto-generates one.  
- Use `key` to reference data independently of position (e.g., database PKs).  

Convert coordinates to cell keys via [`coordinate_to_cell_key`](textual.widgets.DataTable.coordinate_to_cell_key) for coordinate-based operations.

---

### Cursors

Four types: `"cell"` (default), `"row"`, `"column"`, `"none"` — set via `cursor_type` reactive attribute.  
Cursor position exposed as `cursor_coordinate`.

**Keyboard Navigation**:  
- Arrow keys, Page Up/Down, Home, End → move cursor → emit [`CellHighlighted`](textual.widgets.DataTable.CellHighlighted)  
- Enter → select → emit [`CellSelected`](textual.widgets.DataTable.CellSelected)  

For other types:  
- `"row"` → `RowHighlighted`, `RowSelected`  
- `"column"` → `ColumnHighlighted`, `ColumnSelected`

**Mouse Interaction**:  
- Hover → emits `MouseMove`, updates `hover_coordinate`, highlights cell  
- Click → triggers `CellHighlighted` and `CellSelected`

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_cursors.py"
```

---

### Updating Data

Update individual cells via:
- [`update_cell`](textual.widgets.DataTable.update_cell) — by key (row, col)
- [`update_cell_at`](textual.widgets.DataTable.update_cell_at) — by coordinate

---

### Removing Data

- Clear entire table: [`clear`](textual.widgets.DataTable.clear)  
- Remove row by `key`: [`remove_row`](textual.widgets.DataTable.remove_row)  
  ```python
  row_key, _ = table.coordinate_to_cell_key(table.cursor_coordinate)
  table.remove_row(row_key)
  ```
- Remove column by `key`: [`remove_column`](textual.widgets.DataTable.remove_column)  
  ```python
  _, col_key = table.coordinate_to_cell_key(table.cursor_coordinate)
  table.remove_column(col_key)
  ```

---

### Fixed Rows & Columns

Pin rows/columns to top/left via:
- `fixed_rows` (int): number of fixed top rows  
- `fixed_columns` (int): number of fixed left columns  

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_fixed.py"
```

> Example: `fixed_rows=2`, `fixed_columns=1` → first two rows and leftmost column remain visible during scrolling.

---

### Sorting

Sort via [`sort`](textual.widgets.DataTable.sort):

**1. By Column(s)**  
Pass `ColumnKey` or `key` strings (e.g., `"country"`, `"region"`). Sorts by natural order, with secondary sort on ties.

**2. By Key Function**  
Use `key=lambda row: ...` — receives tuple of all values per row; behaves like Python’s `sorted(key=...)`.

**3. Combined Column + Key Function**  
Specify columns in args and use `key` function to refine sorting logic (e.g., limit input size for API calls).

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_renderables.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_cursors.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
# Get the keys for the row and column under the cursor.
row_key, _ = table.coordinate_to_cell_key(table.cursor_coordinate)
# Supply the row key to `remove_row` to delete the row.
table.remove_row(row_key)

```

### `inline_python`

```
# Get the keys for the row and column under the cursor.
_, column_key = table.coordinate_to_cell_key(table.cursor_coordinate)
# Supply the column key to `column_row` to delete the column.
table.remove_column(column_key)

```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_fixed.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_sort.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/data_table_labels.py"

## Messages

#### input.md

**Title:** Input

**Path:** `widgets/input.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Input

A single-line text input widget.

- [x] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

## Examples

### Simple Form
```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/input.py"
```
*Output:* `{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/input.py" press="D,a,r,r,e,n"}`

### Input Types
The `type` parameter restricts input:
- `"integer"`: Integers only  
- `"number"`: Floating-point numbers  
- `"text"`: All text (no restrictions)  

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/input_types.py"
```
*Output:* `{.textual path="docs/examples/input_types.py" press="1234"}`

When `type` ≠ `"text"`, built-in validators apply.

### Restricting Input
Use `restrict=r"[regex]"` to limit characters via full-value regex matching (not per-character).

### Maximum Length
Set `max_length > 0` to cap input length; typing stops at limit.

### Validating Input
Supply one or more `[textual.validation.Validator]` instances. Validation runs on:
- `"changed"`: Value change  
- `"submitted"`: Submit event  
- `"blur"`: Focus loss  

Set `validate_on=["submitted"]` to validate only on submit.

Validation fails if *any* validator fails. Check `event.validation_result` in handlers for `[Input.Changed]`, `[Input.Submitted]`, or `[Input.Blurred]`.

```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/input_validation.py"
```
*Validation Failure:* `{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/input_validation.py" press="-,2,3"}`
*Success:* `{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/input_validation.py" press="4,4"}`

Built-in validators: `Number`, `Function`. Custom via `[Validator]` (e.g., `Palindrome`).

Set `valid_empty=True` to accept empty values without validation.

## Reactive Attributes
| Name              | Type   | Default  | Description                                  |
|-------------------|--------|----------|----------------------------------------------|
| `cursor_blink`    | `bool` | `True`   | Cursor blinking enabled                      |
| `value`           | `str`  | `""`     | Current input value                          |
| `cursor_position` | `int`  | `0`      | Cursor index in string                       |
| `placeholder`     | `str`  | `""`     | Dimmed placeholder when empty                |
| `password`        | `bool` | `False`  | Mask input (password mode)                   |
| `restrict`        | `str`  | `None`   | Regex restricting full value                 |
| `type`            | `str`  | `"text"` | Input type (`"integer"`, `"number"`, `"text"`) |
| `max_length`      | `int`  | `None`   | Max character count                          |
| `valid_empty`     | `bool` | `False`  | Allow empty values to bypass validation      |

## Messages
- `[Input.Blurred]`
- `[Input.Changed]`
- `[Input.Submitted]`

## Bindings
::: textual.widgets.Input.BINDINGS  
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

## Component Classes
::: textual.widgets.Input.COMPONENT_CLASSES  
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

## Additional Notes
Spacing from border; set `border: none;` in CSS to remove.

::: textual.widgets.Input  
    options:
      heading_level: 2

### `inline_python`

```
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/input.py"
    
```

### `inline_python`

    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/input_types.py"

#### masked_input.md

**Title:** MaskedInput

**Path:** `widgets/masked_input.md`

**Content:**

```text
# MaskedInput

!!! tip "Added in version 0.80.0"

A `MaskedInput` derived from `Input`, restricting user input via a template mask and providing visual validation feedback as an implicit *[validator][textual.validation.Validator]*.

- [x] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

## Example

Shows a masked input for credit card number entry (16 digits, grouped in 4s).

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/masked_input.py"}
    ```

=== "masked_input.py"

    ```python hl_lines="6-13 25"
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/masked_input.py"
    ```

> - Textual applies default `-invalid` styling (red border); custom `-valid` styles can be defined (e.g., green border).
> - Template mask defines input format: `#### #### #### ####` for 16-digit credit card.

## Reactive Attributes

| Name       | Type   | Default | Description                     |
|------------|--------|---------|---------------------------------|
| `template` | `str`  | `""`    | Mask template string.           |

### Template Format

Mask length defines max input length. Each character maps to a regex and determines required presence:

| Char | Regex          | Required? |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| `A`  | `[A-Za-z]`     | Yes       |
| `a`  | `[A-Za-z]`     | No        |
| `N`  | `[A-Za-z0-9]`  | Yes       |
| `n`  | `[A-Za-z0-9]`  | No        |
| `X`  | `[^ ]`         | Yes       |
| `x`  | `[^ ]`         | No        |
| `9`  | `[0-9]`        | Yes       |
| `0`  | `[0-9]`        | No        |
| `D`  | `[1-9]`        | Yes       |
| `d`  | `[1-9]`        | No        |
| `#`  | `[0-9+\-]`     | No        |
| `H`  | `[A-Fa-f0-9]`  | Yes       |
| `h`  | `[A-Fa-f0-9]`  | No        |
| `B`  | `[0-1]`        | Yes       |
| `b`  | `[0-1]`        | No        |

Special control chars:
- `>`: Uppercase conversion.
- `<`: Lowercase conversion.
- `!`: Disables case conversion.

All other characters are separators (auto-inserted at position). Escape with `\`.  
Mask may end in `;c`, where `c` is placeholder char. Override via inherited `placeholder`.

## Messages

- [MaskedInput.Changed][textual.widgets.MaskedInput.Changed]
- [MaskedInput.Submitted][textual.widgets.MaskedInput.Submitted]

## Bindings

::: textual.widgets.MaskedInput.BINDINGS
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

## Component Classes

::: textual.widgets.MaskedInput.COMPONENT_CLASSES
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

---  

::: textual.widgets.MaskedInput
    options:
      heading_level: 2
```

# Select

!!! tip "Added in version 0.24.0"

A compact focusable widget for selecting from a list of options.

- [X] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

Options are provided as a sequence of tuples: `(display_label, value)`, where `display_label` is a string or [Rich Renderable](https://rich.readthedocs.io/en/latest/protocol.html). Set via constructor or [`set_options`](textual.widgets.Select.set_options). Current selection stored in `value` attribute and [`Changed`](textual.widgets.Select.Changed) message.

## Typing

Generic type support for option values (e.g., `Select[int]`). Optional; omit if not using typing.

```python
options = [("First", 1), ("Second", 2)]
my_select: Select[int] = Select(options)
```

- `allow_blank: bool = False`  
  If `True`, widget may be unselected. Value becomes [`Select.NULL`](textual.widgets.Select.NULL).  
  - [`is_blank()`](textual.widgets.Select.is_blank): checks blank state  
  - [`clear()`](textual.widgets.Select.clear): sets to blank

## Type-to-Search

#### tabbed_content.md

**Title:** TabbedContent

**Path:** `widgets/tabbed_content.md`

**Content:**

```text
# TabbedContent

!!! tip "Added in version 0.16.0"

Switch between mutually exclusive content panes via a row of tabs.

- [x] Focusable  
- [x] Container  

Combines [`Tabs`](../widgets/tabs.md) and [`ContentSwitcher`](../widgets/content_switcher.md) for navigable content.

Only one child visible at a time; each has an associated tab to toggle visibility.

## Composing

Provide titles via:
1. Positional args in `TabbedContent` constructor:

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    with TabbedContent("Leto", "Jessica", "Paul"):
        yield Markdown(LETO)
        yield Markdown(JESSICA)
        yield Markdown(PAUL)
```

2. Wrapping content in [`TabPane`](textual.widgets.TabPane), which takes title as first arg:

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    with TabbedContent():
        with TabPane("Leto"):
            yield Markdown(LETO)
        with TabPane("Jessica"):
            yield Markdown(JESSICA)
        with TabPane("Paul"):
            yield Markdown(PAUL)
```

## Switching Tabs

Programmatically switch via `id`-assigned `TabPane`s:

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    with TabbedContent():
        with TabPane("Leto", id="leto"):
            yield Markdown(LETO)
        with TabPane("Jessica", id="jessica"):
            yield Markdown(JESSICA)
        with TabPane("Paul", id="paul"):
            yield Markdown(PAUL)

# Switch to Jessica tab
self.query_one(TabbedContent).active = "jessica"
```

> If no `id` provided, panes are auto-assigned IDs: `tab-1`, `tab-2`, etc.

## Initial Tab

Default initial active tab is the first child. Set via `initial` with target `id`:

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    with TabbedContent(initial="jessica"):
        with TabPane("Leto", id="leto"):
            yield Markdown(LETO)
        with TabPane("Jessica", id="jessica"):
            yield Markdown(JESSICA)
        with TabPane("Paul", id="paul"):
            yield Markdown(PAUL)
```

## Example

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/tabbed_content.py"}
    ```

=== "tabbed_content.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/tabbed_content.py"
    ```

## Styling

`TabbedContent` consists of:
- [`Tabs`](tabs.md)  
- [`ContentSwitcher`](content_switcher.md)

Individual tab IDs are prefixed: `--content-tab-{pane_id}`. Use this prefix to style specific tabs.

Example: red/green labels:

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/tabbed_content_label_color.py"}
    ```

=== "tabbed_content.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/tabbed_content_label_color.py"
    ```

## Reactive Attributes

| Name     | Type  | Default | Description                          |
| -------- | ----- | ------- | ------------------------------------ |
| `active` | `str` | `""`    | ID of active tab; set to switch tabs |

## Messages

- [`TabbedContent.Cleared`](textual.widgets.TabbedContent.Cleared)
- [`TabbedContent.TabActivated`](textual.widgets.TabbedContent.TabActivated)

## Bindings

None.

## Component Classes

None.

## See Also

- [Tabs](tabs.md)  
- [ContentSwitcher](content_switcher.md)

---

::: textual.widgets.TabbedContent
    options:
      heading_level: 2

::: textual.widgets.TabPane
    options:
      heading_level: 2

## Embedded Code Examples

#### tabs.md

**Title:** Tabs

**Path:** `widgets/tabs.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Tabs

!!! tip "Added in version 0.15.0"

Displays tab headers that can be activated via click or keyboard navigation.

- [x] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

Construct `Tabs` with positional strings or `[Text][rich.text.Text]` objects to set labels; internally creates `[Tab][textual.widgets.Tab]` instances with auto-incrementing `id`s (`"tab-1"`, `"tab-2"`, etc.). Alternatively, pass `Tab` objects directly to set explicit `id`s.

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    yield Tabs("First tab", "Second tab", Text.from_markup("[u]Third[/u] tab"))
```

```python
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    yield Tabs(
        Tab("First tab", id="one"),
        Tab("Second tab", id="two"),
    )
```

On activation, `Tabs` emits `[Tabs.TabActivated][textual.widgets.Tabs.TabActivated]`, containing the activated `tab`. Access via `event.tab.id`.

## Operations

- **Clear tabs**: Call `[clear][textual.widgets.Tabs.clear]`; triggers `[Tabs.Cleared][textual.widgets.Tabs.Cleared]` with `tab=None`.
- **Add tab(s)**: Use `[add_tab][textual.widgets.Tabs.add_tab]`, accepting strings, `[Text][rich.text.Text]`, or `[Tab][textual.widgets.Tab]`.

## Example

Adds `Tabs` above a label; press `a` to add tabs, `c` to clear.

=== "Output"

    ```{.textual path="docs/examples/widgets/tabs.py" press="a,a,a,a,right,right"}
    ```

=== "tabs.py"

    ```python
    --8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/tabs.py"
    ```

## Reactive Attributes

| Name     | Type  | Default | Description                          |
| -------- | ----- | ------- | ------------------------------------ |
| `active` | `str` | `""`    | ID of active tab; set to switch tabs |

## Messages

- `[Tabs.TabActivated][textual.widgets.Tabs.TabActivated]`
- `[Tabs.Cleared][textual.widgets.Tabs.Cleared]`

## Bindings

::: textual.widgets.Tabs.BINDINGS
    options:
      show_root_heading: false
      show_root_toc_entry: false

## Component Classes

None.

---

::: textual.widgets.Tabs
    options:
      heading_level: 2

---

::: textual.widgets.Tab
    options:
      heading_level: 2

## Embedded Code Examples

### `inline_python`

```
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    yield Tabs("First tab", "Second tab", Text.from_markup("[u]Third[/u] tab"))

```

### `inline_python`

```
def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    yield Tabs(
        Tab("First tab", id="one"),
        Tab("Second tab", id="two"),
    )

```

#### text_area.md

**Title:** TextArea

**Path:** `widgets/text_area.md`

**Content:**

```text
# TextArea

Added in version 0.38.0; soft wrapping added in 0.48.0.

A multi-line text editing widget supporting selection, soft wrapping, optional syntax highlighting via `tree-sitter`, and configurable keybindings.

- [x] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

## Guide

### Code vs Plain Text Editing
By default, `TextArea` is a standard multiline input with soft-wrapping enabled. For code editing, use the [`code_editor`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.code_editor) convenience constructor: returns a `TextArea` with wrapping disabled, line numbers enabled, and tab key inserting `\t`.

### Syntax Highlighting Dependencies
Enable via:
```bash
# pip
pip install "textual[syntax]"

# poetry
poetry add "textual[syntax]"
```
Installs `tree-sitter`, `tree-sitter-languages` (binary wheels). Set [`language`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.language) reactive attribute to enable highlighting.

### Loading Text
Initial content and language:
```python
--8<-- "docs/examples/widgets/text_area_example.py"
```
Update via:
- `text_area.text = "..."` → sets content.
- `text_area.language = "markdown"` → updates parser.

> More languages will be added; custom support available [here](#adding-support-for-custom-languages).

### Reading Content
- [`text`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.text): full text as string.  
- [`selected_text`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.selected_text): selected range.  
- [`get_text_range(start, end)`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.get_text_range): text between locations.  

All return values use the [document line separator](#line-separators).

### Editing Content
- [`replace`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.replace): programmatic paste equivalent.
- [`insert`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.insert), [`delete`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.delete), [`clear`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.clear) → direct edits.

> Use `document.end` for end-of-document location in scripting.

### Cursor & Selection

#### Moving Cursor
- [`cursor_location`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.cursor_location): `(row, col)` zero-based. Assign to move cursor.
```python
>>> text_area = TextArea()
>>> text_area.cursor_location  # (0, 0)
>>> text_area.cursor_location = (0, 4)
>>> text_area.cursor_location  # (0, 4)
```

#### Selecting Text
- [`selection`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.selection): `Selection(start, end)`.  
```python
text_area.selection = Selection((0, 0), (2, 0))  # Selects first two lines.
```
Valid in both directions: `(2, 0)` → `(0, 0)` is equivalent.

> `selection.end` always equals `cursor_location`; `cursor_location` is a convenience accessor.

#### Cursor Utilities

##### Location Info
Properties prefixed with `cursor_at_`:
- [`cursor_at_start_of_line`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.cursor_at_start_of_line): checks if cursor at line start.
- [`get_cursor_right_location`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.get_cursor_right_location): next position on right.

Other variants: `get_cursor_*_location`.

##### Movement Methods
- [`move_cursor`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.move_cursor): move to `(row, col)` with optional selection or centering.
```python
text_area.move_cursor((4, 8), select=True)  # Selects range
```
- [`move_cursor_relative`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.move_cursor_relative): relative movement from current position.

##### Common Selections
- [`select_line`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.select_line): by line index (bound to `F6`).
- [`select_all`](textual.widgets._text_area.TextArea.select_all): selects all text (bound to `F7`).

### Themes

#### Default Theme: `css`
Uses CSS for styling. Integrates with dark/light mode. Style via [component classes](textual.widgets.TextArea.COMPONENT_CLASSES), e.g.:
```css
TextArea .text-area--cursor { background: green; }
```

#### Built-in Themes
Set via `theme` parameter:
```python
yield TextArea.code_editor("print(123)", language="python", theme="dracula")
```
Use `TextAreaTheme` for full customization (syntax, cursor, gutter, etc.).

#### toast.md

**Title:** Toast

**Path:** `widgets/toast.md`

**Content:**

```text
# Toast

!!! tip "Added in version 0.30.0"

A widget displaying a notification message.

- [ ] Focusable  
- [ ] Container  

!!! warning "`Toast` is not intended for direct use; it is consumed by [`notify`](textual.app.App.notify) via Textual's built-in notification system."

## Styling

Customize `Toast` styles using the `Toast` CSS type:

```scss
Toast {
    padding: 3;
}
```

Adjust position via `ToastRack`:

```scss
ToastRack {
    align: right top;
}
```

Severity levels use classes:
- `.toast.-information`
- `.toast.-warning`
- `.toast.-error`

Target specific styles:

```scss
Toast.-information { /* styling */ }
Toast.-warning  { /* styling */ }
Toast.-error   { /* styling */ }
```

Style titles via `toast--title` class (e.g., italic for info):

```scss
Toast.-information .toast--title {
    text-style: italic;
}
```

Tree widgets have a `root` attribute of type [TreeNode][textual.widgets.tree.TreeNode]. Use [add()][textual.widgets.tree.TreeNode.add] or [add_leaf()][textual.widgets.tree.TreeNode.add_leaf] to append child nodes; both return the created `TreeNode`, enabling nested additions.

## Reactive Attributes

| Name          | Type   | Default | Description                     |
| ------------- | ------ | ------- | --------------------------------- |

| `guide_depth` | `int`  | `4`     | Indentation level between parent and child nodes. |

from rich import inspect
from rich.console import Console

c = Console(record=True, width=110)

f = open("foo.txt", "w")

inspect(f, console=c)
c.save_svg("inspect1.svg")

inspect(f, console=c, methods=True)
c.save_svg("inspect2.svg")

inspect(f, console=c, methods=True, help=True)
c.save_svg("inspect3.svg")

#### blocking01.py

**Path:** `blog/snippets/2022-12-07-responsive-app-background-task/blocking01.py`

**Code:**

```python
import time
from random import randint

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.containers import Grid, VerticalScroll
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Footer, Label

class ColourChanger(Widget):  # (1)!
    def on_click(self) -> None:
        self.styles.background = Color(
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
        )

class MyApp(App[None]):
    BINDINGS = [("l", "load", "Load data")]  # (2)!
    CSS = """
    Grid {
        grid-size: 2;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Grid(
            ColourChanger(),
            VerticalScroll(id="log"),
        )
        yield Footer()

    def action_load(self) -> None:  # (3)!
        time.sleep(5)  # (4)!
        self.query_one("#log").mount(Label("Data loaded ✅"))

MyApp().run()

```

#### blocking02.py

**Path:** `blog/snippets/2022-12-07-responsive-app-background-task/blocking02.py`

**Code:**

```python
import asyncio
import time
from random import randint

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.containers import Grid, VerticalScroll
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Footer, Label

class ColourChanger(Widget):
    def on_click(self) -> None:
        self.styles.background = Color(
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
        )

class MyApp(App[None]):
    BINDINGS = [("l", "load", "Load data")]
    CSS = """
    Grid {
        grid-size: 2;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Grid(
            ColourChanger(),
            VerticalScroll(id="log"),
        )
        yield Footer()

    def action_load(self) -> None:  # (1)!
        asyncio.create_task(self._do_long_operation())  # (2)!

    async def _do_long_operation(self) -> None:  # (3)!
        time.sleep(5)
        self.query_one("#log").mount(Label("Data loaded ✅"))

MyApp().run()

```

#### nonblocking01.py

**Path:** `blog/snippets/2022-12-07-responsive-app-background-task/nonblocking01.py`

**Code:**

```python
import asyncio
from random import randint

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.containers import Grid, VerticalScroll
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Footer, Label

class ColourChanger(Widget):
    def on_click(self) -> None:
        self.styles.background = Color(
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
            randint(1, 255),
        )

class MyApp(App[None]):
    BINDINGS = [("l", "load", "Load data")]
    CSS = """
    Grid {
        grid-size: 2;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Grid(
            ColourChanger(),
            VerticalScroll(id="log"),
        )
        yield Footer()

    def action_load(self) -> None:
        asyncio.create_task(self._do_long_operation())

    async def _do_long_operation(self) -> None:
        self.query_one("#log").mount(Label("Starting ⏳"))  # (1)!
        await asyncio.sleep(5)  # (2)!
        self.query_one("#log").mount(Label("Data loaded ✅"))  # (3)!

MyApp().run()

```

### examples

#### event01.py

**Path:** `examples/app/event01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App
from textual import events

class EventApp(App):

    COLORS = [
        "white",
        "maroon",
        "red",
        "purple",
        "fuchsia",
        "olive",
        "yellow",
        "navy",
        "teal",
        "aqua",
    ]

    def on_mount(self) -> None:
        self.screen.styles.background = "darkblue"

    def on_key(self, event: events.Key) -> None:
        if event.key.isdecimal():
            self.screen.styles.background = self.COLORS[int(event.key)]

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = EventApp()
    app.run()

```

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Label, Button

class QuestionApp(App[str]):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label("Do you love Textual?")
        yield Button("Yes", id="yes", variant="primary")
        yield Button("No", id="no", variant="error")

    def on_button_pressed(self, event: Button.Pressed) -> None:
        self.exit(event.button.id)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = QuestionApp()
    reply = app.run()
    print(reply)

#### question_title02.py

**Path:** `examples/app/question_title02.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.events import Key
from textual.widgets import Button, Header, Label

class MyApp(App[str]):
    CSS_PATH = "question02.tcss"
    TITLE = "A Question App"
    SUB_TITLE = "The most important question"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Header()
        yield Label("Do you love Textual?", id="question")
        yield Button("Yes", id="yes", variant="primary")
        yield Button("No", id="no", variant="error")

    def on_button_pressed(self, event: Button.Pressed) -> None:
        self.exit(event.button.id)

    def on_key(self, event: Key):
        self.title = event.key
        self.sub_title = f"You just pressed {event.key}!"

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = MyApp()
    reply = app.run()
    print(reply)

```

#### suspend.py

**Path:** `examples/app/suspend.py`

**Code:**

```python
from os import system

from textual import on
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Button

class SuspendingApp(App[None]):

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Button("Open the editor", id="edit")

    @on(Button.Pressed, "#edit")
    def run_external_editor(self) -> None:
        with self.suspend():  # (1)!
            system("vim")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    SuspendingApp().run()

```

#### custom01.py

**Path:** `examples/events/custom01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.message import Message
from textual.widgets import Static

class ColorButton(Static):
    """A color button."""

    class Selected(Message):
        """Color selected message."""

        def __init__(self, color: Color) -> None:
            self.color = color
            super().__init__()

    def __init__(self, color: Color) -> None:
        self.color = color
        super().__init__()

    def on_mount(self) -> None:
        self.styles.margin = (1, 2)
        self.styles.content_align = ("center", "middle")
        self.styles.background = Color.parse("#ffffff33")
        self.styles.border = ("tall", self.color)

    def on_click(self) -> None:
        # The post_message method sends an event to be handled in the DOM
        self.post_message(self.Selected(self.color))

    def render(self) -> str:
        return str(self.color)

class ColorApp(App):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield ColorButton(Color.parse("#008080"))
        yield ColorButton(Color.parse("#808000"))
        yield ColorButton(Color.parse("#E9967A"))
        yield ColorButton(Color.parse("#121212"))

    def on_color_button_selected(self, message: ColorButton.Selected) -> None:
        self.screen.styles.animate("background", message.color, duration=0.5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ColorApp()
    app.run()

```

import asyncio

try:
    import httpx
except ImportError:
    raise ImportError("Please install httpx with 'pip install httpx' ")

from rich.json import JSON

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import VerticalScroll
from textual.widgets import Input, Static

class DictionaryApp(App):
    """Searches a dictionary API as-you-type."""

    CSS_PATH = "dictionary.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Input(placeholder="Search for a word")
        yield VerticalScroll(Static(id="results"), id="results-container")

    async def on_input_changed(self, message: Input.Changed) -> None:
        """A coroutine to handle a text changed message."""
        if message.value:
            # Look up the word in the background
            asyncio.create_task(self.lookup_word(message.value))
        else:
            # Clear the results
            self.query_one("#results", Static).update()

    async def lookup_word(self, word: str) -> None:
        """Looks up a word."""
        url = f"https://api.dictionaryapi.dev/api/v2/entries/en/{word}"
        async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
            results = (await client.get(url)).text

        if word == self.query_one(Input).value:
            self.query_one("#results", Static).update(JSON(results))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = DictionaryApp()
    app.run()

```

#### on_decorator01.py

**Path:** `examples/events/on_decorator01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Button

class OnDecoratorApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "on_decorator.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        """Three buttons."""
        yield Button("Bell", id="bell")
        yield Button("Toggle dark", classes="toggle dark")
        yield Button("Quit", id="quit")

    def on_button_pressed(self, event: Button.Pressed) -> None:  # (1)!
        """Handle all button pressed events."""
        if event.button.id == "bell":
            self.bell()
        elif event.button.has_class("toggle", "dark"):
            self.theme = (
                "textual-dark" if self.theme == "textual-light" else "textual-light"
            )
        elif event.button.id == "quit":
            self.exit()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = OnDecoratorApp()
    app.run()

```

#### on_decorator02.py

**Path:** `examples/events/on_decorator02.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual import on
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Button

class OnDecoratorApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "on_decorator.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        """Three buttons."""
        yield Button("Bell", id="bell")
        yield Button("Toggle dark", classes="toggle dark")
        yield Button("Quit", id="quit")

    @on(Button.Pressed, "#bell")  # (1)!
    def play_bell(self):
        """Called when the bell button is pressed."""
        self.bell()

    @on(Button.Pressed, ".toggle.dark")  # (2)!
    def toggle_dark(self):
        """Called when the 'toggle dark' button is pressed."""
        self.theme = (
            "textual-dark" if self.theme == "textual-light" else "textual-light"
        )

    @on(Button.Pressed, "#quit")  # (3)!
    def quit(self):
        """Called when the quit button is pressed."""
        self.exit()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = OnDecoratorApp()
    app.run()

```

#### prevent.py

**Path:** `examples/events/prevent.py`

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Button, Input

class PreventApp(App):
    """Demonstrates `prevent` context manager."""

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Input()
        yield Button("Clear", id="clear")

    def on_button_pressed(self) -> None:
        """Clear the text input."""
        input = self.query_one(Input)
        with input.prevent(Input.Changed):  # (1)!
            input.value = ""

    def on_input_changed(self) -> None:
        """Called as the user types."""
        self.bell()  # (2)!

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = PreventApp()
    app.run()

```

#### actions06.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/actions/actions06.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import HorizontalScroll
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widgets import Footer, Placeholder

PAGES_COUNT = 5

class PagesApp(App):
    BINDINGS = [
        ("n", "next", "Next"),
        ("p", "previous", "Previous"),
    ]

    CSS_PATH = "actions06.tcss"

    page_no = reactive(0)

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with HorizontalScroll(id="page-container"):
            for page_no in range(PAGES_COUNT):
                yield Placeholder(f"Page {page_no}", id=f"page-{page_no}")
        yield Footer()

    def action_next(self) -> None:
        self.page_no += 1
        self.refresh_bindings()  # (1)!
        self.query_one(f"#page-{self.page_no}").scroll_visible()

    def action_previous(self) -> None:
        self.page_no -= 1
        self.refresh_bindings()  # (2)!
        self.query_one(f"#page-{self.page_no}").scroll_visible()

    def check_action(
        self, action: str, parameters: tuple[object, ...]
    ) -> bool | None:  # (3)!
        """Check if an action may run."""
        if action == "next" and self.page_no == PAGES_COUNT - 1:
            return False
        if action == "previous" and self.page_no == 0:
            return False
        return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = PagesApp()
    app.run()

```

        ("n", "next", "Next"),

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with HorizontalScroll(id="page-container"):
            for page_no in range(PAGES_COUNT):
                yield Placeholder(f"Page {page_no}", id=f"page-{page_no}")
        yield Footer()

    def action_next(self) -> None:
        self.page_no += 1
        self.query_one(f"#page-{self.page_no}").scroll_visible()

    def action_previous(self) -> None:
        self.page_no -= 1
        self.query_one(f"#page-{self.page_no}").scroll_visible()

    def check_action(self, action: str, parameters: tuple[object, ...]) -> bool | None:
        """Check if an action may run."""
        if action == "next" and self.page_no == PAGES_COUNT - 1:
            return None  # (2)!
        if action == "previous" and self.page_no == 0:
            return None  # (3)!
        return True

if __name__ == "__main__":

from textual._easing import DEFAULT_EASING, EASING
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Static

ease = EASING[DEFAULT_EASING]

class AnimationApp(App):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        self.box = Static("Hello, World!")
        self.box.styles.background = "red"
        self.box.styles.color = "black"
        self.box.styles.padding = (1, 2)
        yield self.box

    def key_1(self):
        self.box.styles.opacity = 1 - ease(0.25)

    def key_2(self):
        self.box.styles.opacity = 1 - ease(0.5)

    def key_3(self):
        self.box.styles.opacity = 1 - ease(0.75)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = AnimationApp()
    app.run()

#### command02.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/command_palette/command02.py`

**Code:**

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from functools import partial
from pathlib import Path

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.command import Hit, Hits, Provider
from textual.containers import VerticalScroll
from textual.widgets import Static

class PythonFileCommands(Provider):
    """A command provider to open a Python file in the current working directory."""

    def read_files(self) -> list[Path]:
        """Get a list of Python files in the current working directory."""
        return list(Path("./").glob("*.py"))

    async def startup(self) -> None:  # (1)!
        """Called once when the command palette is opened, prior to searching."""
        worker = self.app.run_worker(self.read_files, thread=True)
        self.python_paths = await worker.wait()

    async def search(self, query: str) -> Hits:  # (2)!
        """Search for Python files."""
        matcher = self.matcher(query)  # (3)!

        app = self.app
        assert isinstance(app, ViewerApp)

        for path in self.python_paths:
            command = f"open {str(path)}"
            score = matcher.match(command)  # (4)!
            if score > 0:
                yield Hit(
                    score,
                    matcher.highlight(command),  # (5)!
                    partial(app.open_file, path),
                    help="Open this file in the viewer",
                )

class ViewerApp(App):
    """Demonstrate a command source."""

    COMMANDS = App.COMMANDS | {PythonFileCommands}  # (6)!

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with VerticalScroll():
            yield Static(id="code", expand=True)

    def open_file(self, path: Path) -> None:
        """Open and display a file with syntax highlighting."""
        from rich.syntax import Syntax

        syntax = Syntax.from_path(
            str(path),
            line_numbers=True,
            word_wrap=False,
            indent_guides=True,
            theme="github-dark",
        )
        self.query_one("#code", Static).update(syntax)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ViewerApp()
    app.run()

```

#### byte01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/compound/byte01.py`

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import Container
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input, Label, Switch

class BitSwitch(Widget):
    """A Switch with a numeric label above it."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    BitSwitch {
        layout: vertical;
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
    }
    BitSwitch > Label {
        text-align: center;
        width: 100%;
    }
    """

    def __init__(self, bit: int) -> None:
        self.bit = bit
        super().__init__()

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label(str(self.bit))
        yield Switch()

class ByteInput(Widget):
    """A compound widget with 8 switches."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteInput {
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
        border: blank;
        layout: horizontal;
    }
    ByteInput:focus-within {
        border: heavy $secondary;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        for bit in reversed(range(8)):
            yield BitSwitch(bit)

class ByteEditor(Widget):
    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteEditor > Container {
        height: 1fr;
        align: center middle;
    }
    ByteEditor > Container.top {
        background: $boost;
    }
    ByteEditor Input {
        width: 16;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with Container(classes="top"):
            yield Input(placeholder="byte")
        with Container():
            yield ByteInput()

class ByteInputApp(App):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield ByteEditor()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ByteInputApp()
    app.run()

```

#### byte02.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/compound/byte02.py`

**Code:**

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import Container
from textual.message import Message
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input, Label, Switch

class BitSwitch(Widget):
    """A Switch with a numeric label above it."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    BitSwitch {
        layout: vertical;
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
    }
    BitSwitch > Label {
        text-align: center;
        width: 100%;
    }
    """

    class BitChanged(Message):
        """Sent when the 'bit' changes."""

        def __init__(self, bit: int, value: bool) -> None:
            super().__init__()
            self.bit = bit
            self.value = value

    value = reactive(0)  # (1)!

    def __init__(self, bit: int) -> None:
        self.bit = bit
        super().__init__()

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label(str(self.bit))
        yield Switch()

    def on_switch_changed(self, event: Switch.Changed) -> None:  # (2)!
        """When the switch changes, notify the parent via a message."""
        event.stop()  # (3)!
        self.value = event.value  # (4)!
        self.post_message(self.BitChanged(self.bit, event.value))

class ByteInput(Widget):
    """A compound widget with 8 switches."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteInput {
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
        border: blank;
        layout: horizontal;
    }
    ByteInput:focus-within {
        border: heavy $secondary;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        for bit in reversed(range(8)):
            yield BitSwitch(bit)

class ByteEditor(Widget):
    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteEditor > Container {
        height: 1fr;
        align: center middle;
    }
    ByteEditor > Container.top {
        background: $boost;
    }
    ByteEditor Input {
        width: 16;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with Container(classes="top"):
            yield Input(placeholder="byte")
        with Container():
            yield ByteInput()

    def on_bit_switch_bit_changed(self, event: BitSwitch.BitChanged) -> None:
        """When a switch changes, update the value."""
        value = 0
        for switch in self.query(BitSwitch):
            value |= switch.value << switch.bit
        self.query_one(Input).value = str(value)

class ByteInputApp(App):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield ByteEditor()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ByteInputApp()
    app.run()

```

#### byte03.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/compound/byte03.py`

**Code:**

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import Container
from textual.geometry import clamp
from textual.message import Message
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input, Label, Switch

class BitSwitch(Widget):
    """A Switch with a numeric label above it."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    BitSwitch {
        layout: vertical;
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
    }
    BitSwitch > Label {
        text-align: center;
        width: 100%;
    }
    """

    class BitChanged(Message):
        """Sent when the 'bit' changes."""

        def __init__(self, bit: int, value: bool) -> None:
            super().__init__()
            self.bit = bit
            self.value = value

    value = reactive(0)

    def __init__(self, bit: int) -> None:
        self.bit = bit
        super().__init__()

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label(str(self.bit))
        yield Switch()

    def watch_value(self, value: bool) -> None:  # (1)!
        """When the value changes we want to set the switch accordingly."""
        self.query_one(Switch).value = value

    def on_switch_changed(self, event: Switch.Changed) -> None:
        """When the switch changes, notify the parent via a message."""
        event.stop()
        self.value = event.value
        self.post_message(self.BitChanged(self.bit, event.value))

class ByteInput(Widget):
    """A compound widget with 8 switches."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteInput {
        width: auto;
        height: auto;
        border: blank;
        layout: horizontal;
    }
    ByteInput:focus-within {
        border: heavy $secondary;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        for bit in reversed(range(8)):
            yield BitSwitch(bit)

class ByteEditor(Widget):
    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    ByteEditor > Container {
        height: 1fr;
        align: center middle;
    }
    ByteEditor > Container.top {
        background: $boost;
    }
    ByteEditor Input {
        width: 16;
    }
    """

    value = reactive(0)

    def validate_value(self, value: int) -> int:  # (2)!
        """Ensure value is between 0 and 255."""
        return clamp(value, 0, 255)

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with Container(classes="top"):
            yield Input(placeholder="byte")
        with Container():
            yield ByteInput()

    def on_bit_switch_bit_changed(self, event: BitSwitch.BitChanged) -> None:
        """When a switch changes, update the value."""
        value = 0
        for switch in self.query(BitSwitch):
            value |= switch.value << switch.bit
        self.query_one(Input).value = str(value)

    def on_input_changed(self, event: Input.Changed) -> None:  # (3)!
        """When the text changes, set the value of the byte."""
        try:
            self.value = int(event.value or "0")
        except ValueError:
            pass

    def watch_value(self, value: int) -> None:  # (4)!
        """When self.value changes, update switches."""
        for switch in self.query(BitSwitch):
            with switch.prevent(BitSwitch.BitChanged):  # (5)!
                switch.value = bool(value & (1 << switch.bit))  # (6)!

class ByteInputApp(App):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield ByteEditor()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ByteInputApp()
    app.run()

```

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input, Label

class InputWithLabel(Widget):
    """An input with a label."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    InputWithLabel {
        layout: horizontal;
        height: auto;
    }
    InputWithLabel Label {
        padding: 1;
        width: 12;
        text-align: right;
    }
    InputWithLabel Input {
        width: 1fr;
    }
    """

    def __init__(self, input_label: str) -> None:
        self.input_label = input_label
        super().__init__()

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:  # (1)!
        yield Label(self.input_label)
        yield Input()

class CompoundApp(App):
    CSS = """
    Screen {
        align: center middle;
    }
    InputWithLabel {
        width: 80%;
        margin: 1;
    }
    """

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield InputWithLabel("First Name")
        yield InputWithLabel("Last Name")
        yield InputWithLabel("Email")

if __name__ == "__main__":

#### renderables.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/content/renderables.py`

**Code:**

```python
from rich.syntax import Syntax

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult, RenderResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget

class CodeView(Widget):
    """Widget to display Python code."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    CodeView { height: auto; }
    """

    code = reactive("")

    def render(self) -> RenderResult:
        # Syntax is a Rich renderable that displays syntax highlighted code
        syntax = Syntax(self.code, "python", line_numbers=True, indent_guides=True)
        return syntax

class CodeApp(App):
    """App to demonstrate Rich renderables in Textual."""

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        with open(__file__) as self_file:
            code = self_file.read()
        code_view = CodeView()
        code_view.code = code
        yield code_view

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = CodeApp()
    app.run()

```

#### binding01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/input/binding01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.widgets import Footer, Static

class Bar(Static):
    pass

class BindingApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "binding01.tcss"
    BINDINGS = [
        ("r", "add_bar('red')", "Add Red"),
        ("g", "add_bar('green')", "Add Green"),
        ("b", "add_bar('blue')", "Add Blue"),
    ]

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Footer()

    def action_add_bar(self, color: str) -> None:
        bar = Bar(color)
        bar.styles.background = Color.parse(color).with_alpha(0.5)
        self.mount(bar)
        self.call_after_refresh(self.screen.scroll_end, animate=False)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = BindingApp()
    app.run()

```

class InputApp(App):

        yield RichLog()

from textual import events
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import RichLog

class KeyLogger(RichLog):
    def on_key(self, event: events.Key) -> None:
        self.write(event)

class InputApp(App):
    """App to display key events."""

    CSS_PATH = "key03.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield KeyLogger()
        yield KeyLogger()

#### mouse01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/input/mouse01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual import events
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import RichLog, Static

class Ball(Static):
    pass

class MouseApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "mouse01.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield RichLog()
        yield Ball("Textual")

    def on_mouse_move(self, event: events.MouseMove) -> None:
        self.screen.query_one(RichLog).write(event)
        self.query_one(Ball).offset = event.screen_offset - (8, 2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = MouseApp()
    app.run()

```

#### combining_layouts.py

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import Container, Horizontal, VerticalScroll
from textual.widgets import Header, Static

class CombiningLayoutsExample(App):
    CSS_PATH = "combining_layouts.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Header()
        with Container(id="app-grid"):
            with VerticalScroll(id="left-pane"):
                for number in range(15):
                    yield Static(f"Vertical layout, child {number}")
            with Horizontal(id="top-right"):
                yield Static("Horizontally")
                yield Static("Positioned")
                yield Static("Children")
                yield Static("Here")
            with Container(id="bottom-right"):
                yield Static("This")
                yield Static("panel")
                yield Static("is")
                yield Static("using")
                yield Static("grid layout!", id="bottom-right-final")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = CombiningLayoutsExample()
    app.run()

```

#### dock_layout1_sidebar.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/layout/dock_layout1_sidebar.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.widgets import Static

TEXT = """\
Docking a widget removes it from the layout and fixes its position, aligned to either the top, right, bottom, or left edges of a container.

Docked widgets will not scroll out of view, making them ideal for sticky headers, footers, and sidebars.

"""

class DockLayoutExample(App):
    CSS_PATH = "dock_layout1_sidebar.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Static("Sidebar", id="sidebar")
        yield Static(TEXT * 10, id="body")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = DockLayoutExample()
    app.run()

```

#### computed01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/computed01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.color import Color
from textual.containers import Horizontal
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widgets import Input, Static

class ComputedApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "computed01.tcss"

    red = reactive(0)
    green = reactive(0)
    blue = reactive(0)
    color = reactive(Color.parse("transparent"))

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Horizontal(
            Input("0", placeholder="Enter red 0-255", id="red"),
            Input("0", placeholder="Enter green 0-255", id="green"),
            Input("0", placeholder="Enter blue 0-255", id="blue"),
            id="color-inputs",
        )
        yield Static(id="color")

    def compute_color(self) -> Color:  # (1)!
        return Color(self.red, self.green, self.blue).clamped

    def watch_color(self, color: Color) -> None:  # (2)
        self.query_one("#color").styles.background = color

    def on_input_changed(self, event: Input.Changed) -> None:
        try:
            component = int(event.value)
        except ValueError:
            self.bell()
        else:
            if event.input.id == "red":
                self.red = component
            elif event.input.id == "green":
                self.green = component
            else:
                self.blue = component

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = ComputedApp()
    app.run()

```

#### dynamic_watch.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/dynamic_watch.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Button, Label, ProgressBar

class Counter(Widget):
    DEFAULT_CSS = "Counter { height: auto; }"
    counter = reactive(0)  # (1)!

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label()
        yield Button("+10")

    def on_button_pressed(self) -> None:
        self.counter += 10

    def watch_counter(self, counter_value: int):
        self.query_one(Label).update(str(counter_value))

class WatchApp(App[None]):
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Counter()
        yield ProgressBar(total=100, show_eta=False)

    def on_mount(self):
        def update_progress(counter_value: int):  # (2)!
            self.query_one(ProgressBar).update(progress=counter_value)

        self.watch(self.query_one(Counter), "counter", update_progress)  # (3)!

if __name__ == "__main__":
    WatchApp().run()

```

#### recompose01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/recompose01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from datetime import datetime

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widgets import Digits

class Clock(App):

    CSS = """
    Screen {align: center middle}
    Digits {width: auto}
    """

    time: reactive[datetime] = reactive(datetime.now, init=False)

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Digits(f"{self.time:%X}")

    def watch_time(self) -> None:  # (1)!
        self.query_one(Digits).update(f"{self.time:%X}")

    def update_time(self) -> None:
        self.time = datetime.now()

    def on_mount(self) -> None:
        self.set_interval(1, self.update_time)  # (2)!

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = Clock()
    app.run()

```

#### recompose02.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/recompose02.py`

**Code:**

```python
from datetime import datetime

from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widgets import Digits

class Clock(App):

    CSS = """
    Screen {align: center middle}
    Digits {width: auto}
    """

    time: reactive[datetime] = reactive(datetime.now, recompose=True)

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Digits(f"{self.time:%X}")

    def update_time(self) -> None:
        self.time = datetime.now()

    def on_mount(self) -> None:
        self.set_interval(1, self.update_time)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = Clock()
    app.run()

```

#### refresh01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/refresh01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input

class Name(Widget):
    """Generates a greeting."""

    who = reactive("name")

    def render(self) -> str:
        return f"Hello, {self.who}!"

class WatchApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "refresh01.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Input(placeholder="Enter your name")
        yield Name()

    def on_input_changed(self, event: Input.Changed) -> None:
        self.query_one(Name).who = event.value

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WatchApp()
    app.run()

```

#### refresh03.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/refresh03.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.reactive import reactive
from textual.widget import Widget
from textual.widgets import Input, Label

class Name(Widget):
    """Generates a greeting."""

    who = reactive("name", recompose=True)  # (1)!

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:  # (2)!
        yield Label(f"Hello, {self.who}!")

class WatchApp(App):
    CSS_PATH = "refresh02.tcss"

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Input(placeholder="Enter your name")
        yield Name()

    def on_input_changed(self, event: Input.Changed) -> None:
        self.query_one(Name).who = event.value

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WatchApp()
    app.run()

```

#### set_reactive01.py

**Path:** `examples/guide/reactivity/set_reactive01.py`

**Code:**

```python
from textual.app import App, ComposeResult
from textual.containers import Horizontal
from textual.reactive import reactive, var
from textual.widgets import Label

GREETINGS = [
    "Bonjour",
    "Hola",
    "こんにちは",
    "你好",
    "안녕하세요",
    "Hello",
]

class Greeter(Horizontal):
    """Display a greeting and a name."""

    DEFAULT_CSS = """
    Greeter {
        width: auto;
        height: 1;
        & Label {
            margin: 0 1;
        }
    }
    """
    greeting: reactive[str] = reactive("")
    who: reactive[str] = reactive("")

    def __init__(self, greeting: str = "Hello", who: str = "World!") -> None:
        super().__init__()
        self.greeting = greeting  # (1)!
        self.who = who

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Label(self.greeting, id="greeting")
        yield Label(self.who, id="name")

    def watch_greeting(self, greeting: str) -> None:
        self.query_one("#greeting", Label).update(greeting)  # (2)!

    def watch_who(self, who: str) -> None:
        self.query_one("#who", Label).update(who)

class NameApp(App):

    CSS = """
    Screen {
        align: center middle;
    }
    """
    greeting_no: var[int] = var(0)
    BINDINGS = [("space", "greeting")]

    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Greeter(who="Textual")

    def action_greeting(self) -> None:
        self.greeting_no = (self.greeting_no + 1) % len(GREETINGS)
        self.query_one(Greeter).greeting = GREETINGS[self.greeting_no]

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = NameApp()
    app.run()

```
